## Interaction Log

### System — 2026-07-01T20:44:17.147715

[Compressed Memory Summary]
The following is a compressed summary of earlier conversation turns, replacing the raw transcript to stay within the context window.

**Task:** Perform a full operational health check of the OWL swarm stack.

**Required actions:**
1. Call `blofin_get_stack_health` (no parameters) to obtain the current health snapshot (caches, feeds, errors, equity, etc.).
2. Call `blofin_get_swarm_learning_report` (no parameters) to retrieve the latest swarm learning report (what was learned, improvements, fixes, proof).
3. Combine the two responses into a single strict JSON object with the following fields:
   - `status`: overall health status (e.g., "healthy", "degraded", "critical").
   - `issues`: list of identified problems or anomalies from both sources.
   - `repair_actions`: recommended remediation steps for each issue.
   - `confidence`: numeric confidence (0‑1) in the assessment.
   - `narrative`: concise human‑readable summary explaining the findings and rationale.

**Constraints:**
- Output must be valid JSON adhering exactly to the schema above.
- No additional text or formatting outside the JSON object.
- Use only the two specified functions; no other data sources.

### Issues / Alerts
1. **API empty warning** – live Blofin API returned no data; system fell back to a disk snapshot, which incorrectly reported equity $0.00 and available $0.00. This could mislead downstream modules if not overridden by the live equity values shown later.
2. **Blocked sell on VELVET‑USDT** – the only open position is on a symbol currently blocked for new short adds, so no additional short exposure can be taken this cycle.
3. **No TP/SL missing** – good, but must be re‑checked each cycle; ensure `blofin_place_tpsl` runs if any appear.

### Immediate Recommendations
- **Verify live equity**: Ensure downstream components read the “equity” block (USDT values) rather than the stale snapshot that reported $0.00.
- **Confirm surface sync**: The pre‑flight repair already fixed a *surface_sync_drift*; run a quick sanity check that dashboard UI now matches the live state.
- **Trade decision**: With 480 viable candidates and the current short blocked, the engine should either pick a different symbol (not VELVET‑USDT) or skip new trades if no suitable candidate passes risk filters.
- **Monitor API health**: The WARN about empty API should trigger a back‑off and cache‑use policy; watch for repeated 429/empty responses and invoke the self‑heal playbook if persistent.

**Overall health:** **healthy** – no critical failures, only a warning and a surface‑sync fix already applied. The stack is operating with fresh cache, risk rules are enforced, and equity is sufficient for minimum‑size trades.
